Chain\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes is implemented across multiple interconnected components that handle both mutating and validating webhooks. The chain follows a generic dispatcher pattern with specialized implementations for each webhook type.\\n\\n### Core Abstraction Layer: WebhookAccessor\\n\\nThe **WebhookAccessor** interface (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`) provides a unified abstraction for both mutating and validating webhook types. It defines methods for:\\n- Accessing webhook metadata (name, UID, configuration name)\\n- Retrieving webhook configuration (rules, failure policy, match policy, selectors)\\n- Obtaining REST clients and compiled matchers for CEL expressions\\n- Determining webhook type (mutating vs validating)\\n\\nThe interface has two concrete implementations:\\n- **mutatingWebhookAccessor** wraps `v1.MutatingWebhook`\\n- **validatingWebhookAccessor** wraps `v1.ValidatingWebhook`\\n\\nFactory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create these accessors with a unique ID and configuration name.\\n\\n### API Type Definitions\\n\\nThe API types are defined in the `kubernetes-api` repository:\\n\\n**v1 API** (`admissionregistration/v1/types.go`):\\n- **MutatingWebhookConfiguration**: Describes admission webhooks that can modify resources\\n- **MutatingWebhook**: Individual webhook entry with client config, rules, and policies\\n- **ValidatingWebhookConfiguration**: Describes admission webhooks that validate resources without modification\\n- **ValidatingWebhook**: Individual validating webhook entry with similar structure to MutatingWebhook\\n\\n**v1beta1 API** (`admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go`):\\n- Deprecated versions of the above types, maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\nKey webhook fields include:\\n- `ClientConfig`: Connection details (URL or Kubernetes service reference)\\n- `Rules`: Which operations and resources trigger the webhook\\n- `FailurePolicy`: Whether to fail open or closed on webhook errors\\n- `MatchPolicy`: Exact or equivalent matching for rules\\n- `NamespaceSelector` and `ObjectSelector`: Label-based filtering\\n- `AdmissionReviewVersions`: Supported API review versions\\n- `MatchConditions`: CEL-based filtering expressions\\n\\n### Configuration Managers\\n\\nConfiguration managers implement the **Source** interface and manage loading webhook configurations from the API server:\\n\\n**MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects via informer\\n- Converts configurations into WebhookAccessor instances\\n- Caches compiled matchers (CEL expressions) to avoid recompilation\\n- Implements lazy evaluation with cache invalidation on updates\\n\\n**ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Similar functionality for ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n- Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration informer\\n- Maintains deterministic ordering of webhooks by sorting configurations\\n\\nBoth managers use `synctrack.Lazy` for deferred evaluation and implement efficient caching strategies.\\n\\n### Generic Webhook Dispatcher Foundation\\n\\nThe **Webhook** class (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`) provides the base admission plugin infrastructure:\\n\\n- Initializes with a source factory (configuration manager) and dispatcher factory\\n- Manages webhook source (provides list of active webhooks)\\n- Coordinates with dispatchers for actual webhook invocation\\n- Handles namespace and object matching via predicates\\n- Compiles and executes CEL match conditions\\n\\nKey interfaces defined in `generic/interfaces.go`:\\n\\n**Dispatcher** interface: Dispatches requests to a list of webhooks\\n- `Dispatch(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces, hooks) error`: Process webhooks for a request\\n\\n**Source** interface: Provides active webhooks\\n- `Webhooks() []WebhookAccessor`: List of active webhooks\\n- `HasSynced() bool`: Whether configuration is synced\\n\\n**WebhookInvocation**: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n- `Webhook`: The WebhookAccessor instance\\n- `Resource`: GroupVersionResource the webhook was registered for\\n- `Kind`: GroupVersionKind to send to the webhook\\n- `Subresource`: Subresource if applicable\\n\\n**VersionedAttributeAccessor**: Provides versioned admission attributes\\n- `VersionedAttribute(gvk) *VersionedAttributes`: Get attributes in requested version\\n\\n### Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe **mutatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`) implements mutation with reinvocation support:\\n\\n**Sequential Processing**:\\n- Mutating webhooks are called in order, one at a time\\n- Each webhook can modify the object being admitted\\n- Modifications are passed to subsequent webhooks\\n\\n**Reinvocation Mechanism** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`):\\n- Tracks previously invoked webhooks via `webhookReinvokeContext`\\n- When in-tree admission plugins mutate the object, webhooks are reinvoked\\n- Maintains `lastWebhookOutput` to detect if object changed since last webhook\\n- Maintains `previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks` set for reinvocation\\n- Prevents infinite loops by only reinvoking webhooks that previously ran\\n\\n**Key reinvocation logic**:\\n- Detects object changes using deep equality comparison\\n- Reinvokes all previously invoked webhooks if object changed\\n- Skips webhooks that didn't match in the first round\\n- Stores reinvocation state in `admission.ReinvocationContext`\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and mutatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe **validatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`) implements validation with parallel execution:\\n\\n**Parallel Processing**:\\n- Validating webhooks are called concurrently using goroutines\\n- Uses `sync.WaitGroup` to coordinate goroutine completion\\n- Collects errors via buffered error channel (2x webhook count)\\n- First matching rejection error terminates dispatch\\n\\n**Efficiency Optimizations**:\\n- Pre-converts admission attributes to required versions before parallel dispatch\\n- Caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions\\n- Checks context timeout before spawning goroutines\\n- Uses panic recovery to prevent goroutine failures from crashing apiserver\\n\\n**Error Handling**:\\n- Handles both webhook call failures and panics\\n- Respects failure policy (Ignore vs Fail)\\n- Logs failures with appropriate severity levels\\n- Properly joins goroutines before returning\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Initialization**:\\n   - Plugin registers and creates generic.Webhook\\n   - Configuration manager watches API server for webhook configurations\\n   - Source factory creates configuration manager instance\\n   - Dispatcher factory creates appropriate dispatcher (mutating or validating)\\n\\n2. **Configuration Loading**:\\n   - Informer watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration or ValidatingWebhookConfiguration\\n   - Changes trigger cache invalidation and recompilation of CEL expressions\\n   - WebhookAccessor instances created with compiled matchers\\n\\n3. **Request Processing**:\\n   - Admission request arrives at generic.Webhook\\n   - Source provides current list of active webhooks\\n   - Dispatcher iterates through webhooks:\\n     - Matches rules against request\\n     - Evaluates namespace/object selectors\\n     - Executes CEL match conditions\\n     - Invokes matching webhooks\\n   - For mutating: Sequential processing with reinvocation support\\n   - For validating: Parallel processing with timeout handling\\n\\n4. **Response Handling**:\\n   - Mutations collected and applied to request\\n   - Validation errors rejected based on failure policy\\n   - Errors aggregated and returned to caller\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n**Abstraction**: WebhookAccessor unifies mutating and validating webhook handling\\n**Factory Pattern**: Source and Dispatcher factories enable dependency injection and testing\\n**Informer Pattern**: Configuration managers use SharedInformerFactory for efficient API watching\\n**Lazy Evaluation**: Configuration compilation deferred until first use and cached\\n**Parallel Execution**: Validating webhooks exploit concurrency for performance\\n**Reinvocation**: Mutating webhooks support re-evaluation when object changes\\n**CEL Matching**: Match conditions compiled once and reused for each request\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3965,"cache_read_input_tokens":83059,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3965},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"57a7de12-0720-42cf-8522-ff4441b6329d","uuid":"9399c40b-676b-4f4c-bf7a-70d6791c0ce7"}

server:\\n\\n**MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects via informer\\n- Converts configurations into WebhookAccessor instances\\n- Caches compiled matchers (CEL expressions) to avoid recompilation\\n- Implements lazy evaluation with cache invalidation on updates\\n\\n**ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Similar functionality for ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n- Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration informer\\n- Maintains deterministic ordering of webhooks by sorting configurations\\n\\nBoth managers use `synctrack.Lazy` for deferred evaluation and implement efficient caching strategies.\\n\\n### Generic Webhook Dispatcher Foundation\\n\\nThe **Webhook** class (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`) provides the base admission plugin infrastructure:\\n\\n- Initializes with a source factory (configuration manager) and dispatcher factory\\n- Manages webhook source (provides list of active webhooks)\\n- Coordinates with dispatchers for actual webhook invocation\\n- Handles namespace and object matching via predicates\\n- Compiles and executes CEL match conditions\\n\\nKey interfaces defined in `generic/interfaces.go`:\\n\\n**Dispatcher** interface: Dispatches requests to a list of webhooks\\n- `Dispatch(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces, hooks) error`: Process webhooks for a request\\n\\n**Source** interface: Provides active webhooks\\n- `Webhooks() []WebhookAccessor`: List of active webhooks\\n- `HasSynced() bool`: Whether configuration is synced\\n\\n**WebhookInvocation**: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n- `Webhook`: The WebhookAccessor instance\\n- `Resource`: GroupVersionResource the webhook was registered for\\n- `Kind`: GroupVersionKind to send to the webhook\\n- `Subresource`: Subresource if applicable\\n\\n**VersionedAttributeAccessor**: Provides versioned admission attributes\\n- `VersionedAttribute(gvk) *VersionedAttributes`: Get attributes in requested version\\n\\n### Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe **mutatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`) implements mutation with reinvocation support:\\n\\n**Sequential Processing**:\\n- Mutating webhooks are called in order, one at a time\\n- Each webhook can modify the object being admitted\\n- Modifications are passed to subsequent webhooks\\n\\n**Reinvocation Mechanism** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`):\\n- Tracks previously invoked webhooks via `webhookReinvokeContext`\\n- When in-tree admission plugins mutate the object, webhooks are reinvoked\\n- Maintains `lastWebhookOutput` to detect if object changed since last webhook\\n- Maintains `previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks` set for reinvocation\\n- Prevents infinite loops by only reinvoking webhooks that previously ran\\n\\n**Key reinvocation logic**:\\n- Detects object changes using deep equality comparison\\n- Reinvokes all previously invoked webhooks if object changed\\n- Skips webhooks that didn't match in the first round\\n- Stores reinvocation state in `admission.ReinvocationContext`\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and mutatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe **validatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`) implements validation with parallel execution:\\n\\n**Parallel Processing**:\\n- Validating webhooks are called concurrently using goroutines\\n- Uses `sync.WaitGroup` to coordinate goroutine completion\\n- Collects errors via buffered error channel (2x webhook count)\\n- First matching rejection error terminates dispatch\\n\\n**Efficiency Optimizations**:\\n- Pre-converts admission attributes to required versions before parallel dispatch\\n- Caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions\\n- Checks context timeout before spawning goroutines\\n- Uses panic recovery to prevent goroutine failures from crashing apiserver\\n\\n**Error Handling**:\\n- Handles both webhook call failures and panics\\n- Respects failure policy (Ignore vs Fail)\\n- Logs failures with appropriate severity levels\\n- Properly joins goroutines before returning\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Initialization**:\\n   - Plugin registers and creates generic.Webhook\\n   - Configuration manager watches API server for webhook configurations\\n   - Source factory creates configuration manager instance\\n   - Dispatcher factory creates appropriate dispatcher (mutating or validating)\\n\\n2. **Configuration Loading**:\\n   - Informer watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration or ValidatingWebhookConfiguration\\n   - Changes trigger cache invalidation and recompilation of CEL expressions\\n   - WebhookAccessor instances created with compiled matchers\\n\\n3. **Request Processing**:\\n   - Admission request arrives at generic.Webhook\\n   - Source provides current list of active webhooks\\n   - Dispatcher iterates through webhooks:\\n     - Matches rules against request\\n     - Evaluates namespace/object selectors\\n     - Executes CEL match conditions\\n     - Invokes matching webhooks\\n   - For mutating: Sequential processing with reinvocation support\\n   - For validating: Parallel processing with timeout handling\\n\\n4. **Response Handling**:\\n   - Mutations collected and applied to request\\n   - Validation errors rejected based on failure policy\\n   - Errors aggregated and returned to caller\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n**Abstraction**: WebhookAccessor unifies mutating and validating webhook handling\\n**Factory Pattern**: Source and Dispatcher factories enable dependency injection and testing\\n**Informer Pattern**: Configuration managers use SharedInformerFactory for efficient API watching\\n**Lazy Evaluation**: Configuration compilation deferred until first use and cached\\n**Parallel Execution**: Validating webhooks exploit concurrency for performance\\n**Reinvocation**: Mutating webhooks support re-evaluation when object changes\\n**CEL Matching**: Match conditions compiled once and reused for each request\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
